  <p>\n                  <strong>Hari \xc5\x9bara\xe1\xb9\x87am</strong> means <em>Hari is refuge</em>. document.documentElement.scrollHeight - window.innerHeight;\n          const ratio = docHeight > 0 ? Math.min(scrollTop / docHeight, 1) : 0;\n          progress.style.width = `${ratio * 100}%`;\n        }\n\n        updateProgress();\n        window.addEventListener("scroll", updateProgress, { passive: true });\n\n        if (reduceMotion) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        let rafId = null;\n        let pointerX = window.innerWidth / 2;\n        let pointerY = window.innerHeight / 2;\n\n        function applyParallax() {\n          rafId = null;\n          const offsetX = (pointerX / window.innerWidth - 0.5) * 2;\n          const offsetY = (pointerY / window.innerHeight - 0.5) * 2;\n\n          if (aura) {\n            aura.style.left = `${pointerX}px`;\n            aura.style.top = `${pointerY}px`;\n          }\n\n          parallaxNodes.forEach((node) => {\n            const depth = Number(node.dataset.depth || 8);\n            node.style.transform = `translate3d(${offsetX * depth}px, ${offsetY * depth}px, 0)`;\n          });\n        }\n\n        function requestParallax() {\n          if (rafId !== null) {\n            return;\n          }\n          rafId = window.requestAnimationFrame(applyParallax);\n        }\n\n        window.addEventListener("mousemove", (event) => {\n          pointerX = event.clientX;\n          pointerY = event.clientY;\n          requestParallax();\n        }, { passive: true });\n\n        window.addEventListener("mouseleave", () => {\n          if (aura) {\n            aura.style.opacity = "0";\n          }\n        });\n\n        window.addEventListener("mouseenter", () => {\n          if (aura) {\n            aura.style.opacity = "";\n          }\n        });\n      }\n\n      function scrollTranscriptToLatest() {\n        const transcript = document.querySelector("[data-transcript]");\n        if (transcript) {\n          transcript.scrollTop = transcript.scrollHeight;\n        }\n      }\n\n      function scrollTranscriptToLatestReplyStart() {\n        const transcript = document.querySelector("[data-transcript]");\n        if (!transcript) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        const assistantBubbles = transcript.querySelectorAll(".chat-bubble.assistant");\n        const latestAssistant = assistantBubbles[assistantBubbles.length - 1];\n        if (!latestAssistant) {\n          scrollTranscriptToLatest();\n          return;\n        }\n\n        const topOffset = latestAssistant.offsetTop - 12;\n        transcript.scrollTop = Math.max(topOffset, 0);\n      }\n\n      function scrollToUserBubbleInTranscript() {\n        // Scroll inside the transcript container to show the user\'s newest message\n        const transcript = document.querySelector("[data-transcript]");\n        if (!transcript) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        const userBubbles = transcript.querySelectorAll(".chat-bubble.user");\n        const latestUser = userBubbles[userBubbles.length - 1];\n        if (latestUser) {\n          const topOffset = latestUser.offsetTop - 12;\n          transcript.scrollTop = Math.max(topOffset, 0);\n          // Also bring the transcript into the viewport\n          latestUser.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "auto", block: "nearest" });\n        }\n      }\n\n      function scrollToLatestAssistantInTranscript() {\n        // Scroll inside the transcript container so the newest assistant reply is visible\n        const transcript = document.querySelector("[data-transcript]");\n        if (!transcript) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        const assistantBubbles = transcript.querySelectorAll(".chat-bubble.assistant");\n        const latestAssistant = assistantBubbles[assistantBubbles.length - 1];\n        if (latestAssistant) {\n          const topOffset = latestAssistant.offsetTop - 12;\n          transcript.scrollTop = Math.max(topOffset, 0);\n          // Also bring the assistant bubble into the page viewport\n          latestAssistant.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "auto", block: "nearest" });\n        } else {\n          scrollTranscriptToLatest();\n        }\n      }\n\n      const forms = document.querySelectorAll(".quick-submit");\n      forms.forEach((form) => {\n        if (form.dataset.quickBound === "true") {\n          return;\n        }\n        form.dataset.quickBound = "true";\n        form.addEventListener("submit", () => {\n          form.classList.add("loading");\n        });\n      });\n\n      function animateTyping(container, speed) {\n        if (!container) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        const textNode = container.querySelector(".typing-text");\n        const cursorNode = container.querySelector(".typing-cursor");\n        if (!textNode || !cursorNode) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        const fullText = textNode.textContent || "";\n        textNode.textContent = "";\n        let index = 0;\n\n        // Only animate the newest assistant output so revisiting a thread\n        // keeps older history instantly readable for the user.\n        function tick() {\n          if (index >= fullText.length) {\n            textNode.textContent = fullText;\n            cursorNode.remove();\n            container.classList.remove("typing-live");\n            return;\n          }\n\n          const step = fullText[index] === " " ? 1 : Math.min(2, fullText.length - index);\n          textNode.textContent += fullText.slice(index, index + step);\n          index += step;\n          window.setTimeout(\n            tick,\n            fullText[index - 1] === " " ? speed / 2 : speed,\n          );\n        }\n\n        tick();\n      }\n\n      animateTyping(\n        document.querySelector(\'[data-typing-target="latest-reply"]\'),\n        18,\n      );\n      animateTyping(\n        document.querySelector(\'[data-typing-target="guidance-panel"]\'),\n        11,\n      );\n\n      function buildBubble(role, contentHtml) {\n        const currentLanguage = (\n          document.querySelector("#sidebar_language")?.value\n          || document.querySelector(\'input[name="language"]\')?.value\n          || "en"\n        );\n        const bubble = document.createElement("div");\n        bubble.className = `chat-bubble ${role}`;\n\n        const label = document.createElement("span");\n        label.className = "chat-role";\n        if (role === "user") {\n          label.textContent = currentLanguage === "hi" ? "\xe0\xa4\x86\xe0\xa4\xaa" : "You";\n        } else {\n          label.textContent = (\n            currentLanguage === "hi"\n              ? "\xe0\xa4\xae\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa4\xb0\xe0\xa5\x8d\xe0\xa4\x97\xe0\xa4\xa6\xe0\xa4\xb0\xe0\xa5\x8d\xe0\xa4\xb6\xe0\xa4\xa8"\n              : "Guide"\n          );\n        }\n        bubble.appendChild(label);\n\n        const content = document.createElement("div");\n        content.innerHTML = contentHtml;\n        bubble.appendChild(content);\n        if (window.gsap) {\n          window.gsap.fromTo(\n            bubble,\n            { y: 8, opacity: 0 },\n            { y: 0, opacity: 1, duration: 0.22, ease: "power1.out" },\n          );\n        }\n        return bubble;\n      }\n\n      function ensureTranscript() {\n        let transcript = document.querySelector("[data-transcript]");\n        if (transcript) {\n          return transcript;\n        }\n\n        const chatShell = document.querySelector(".chat-shell");\n        if (!chatShell) {\n          return null;\n        }\n\n        const scrollArea = chatShell.querySelector(".chat-scroll-area");\n        if (!scrollArea) {\n          return null;\n        }\n\n        transcript = document.createElement("div");\n        transcript.className = "transcript";\n        transcript.setAttribute("data-transcript", "");\n        scrollArea.appendChild(transcript);\n        return transcript;\n      }\n\n      function replaceAppFromHtml(html, nextUrl) {\n        const parser = new DOMParser();\n        const doc = parser.parseFromString(html, "text/html");\n        const nextApp = doc.querySelector("main.app");\n        const currentApp = document.querySelector("main.app");\n\n        if (!nextApp || !currentApp) {\n          window.location.reload();\n          return false;\n        }\n\n        currentApp.replaceWith(nextApp);\n        if (nextUrl) {\n          window.history.replaceState({}, "", nextUrl);\n        }\n        if (typeof window.initChatUi === "function") {\n          window.initChatUi();\n        }\n        return true;\n      }\n\n      async function handleLiveAsk(form) {\n        const transcript = ensureTranscript();\n        if (!transcript) {\n          form.submit();\n          return;\n        }\n\n        const formData = new FormData(form);\n        const action = String(formData.get("action") || "");\n        if (action !== "ask") {\n          form.submit();\n          return;\n        }\n\n        const message = String(formData.get("message") || "").trim();\n        if (!message) {\n          form.submit();\n          return;\n        }\n\n        form.classList.add("loading");\n\n        if (typeof window.postAnalyticsEvent === "function") {\n          window.postAnalyticsEvent({\n            event_type: "ask_submit",\n            source: "chat_ui",\n            path: window.location.pathname,\n            metadata: {\n              mode: String(formData.get("mode") || "simple"),\n              language: String(formData.get("language") || "en"),\n            },\n          });\n        }\n\n        const emptyState = transcript.querySelector(".transcript-empty");\n        if (emptyState) {\n          emptyState.remove();\n        }\n\n        // Show the user\'s new message immediately so the chat feels live,\n        // then keep a thinking bubble in place until the server reply arrives.\n        const userBubble = buildBubble(\n          "user",\n          message.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;"),\n        );\n        userBubble.setAttribute("data-live-user", "true");\n        transcript.appendChild(userBubble);\n        const thinkingBubble = buildBubble(\n          "assistant",\n          (\n            \'<div class="thinking-bubble">\'\n            + \'<div class="chakra-loader-wrap">\'\n            + \'<span class="chakra-loader" aria-hidden="true"></span>\'\n            + \'<span class="chakra-caption">\'\n            + (\n              (document.querySelector("#sidebar_language")?.value || "en") === "hi"\n                ? "\xe0\xa4\xa6\xe0\xa4\xbf\xe0\xa4\xb5\xe0\xa5\x8d\xe0\xa4\xaf \xe0\xa4\xae\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa4\xb0\xe0\xa5\x8d\xe0\xa4\x97\xe0\xa4\xa6\xe0\xa4\xb0\xe0\xa5\x8d\xe0\xa4\xb6\xe0\xa4\xa8 \xe0\xa4\xaa\xe0\xa5\x8d\xe0\xa4\xb0\xe0\xa4\x95\xe0\xa4\x9f \xe0\xa4\xb9\xe0\xa5\x8b \xe0\xa4\xb0\xe0\xa4\xb9\xe0\xa4\xbe \xe0\xa4\xb9\xe0\xa5\x88..."\n                : "Receiving divine guidance..."\n            )\n            + \'</span>\'\n            + "</div>"\n            + "</div>"\n          ),\n        );\n        transcript.appendChild(thinkingBubble);\n\n        // Clear the textarea immediately after sending\n        const textarea = form.querySelector("textarea[name=\'message\']");\n        if (textarea) {\n          textarea.value = "";\n        }\n\n        // Keep the newest waiting state (Sudarshan loader) in view\n        // so users never need to manually scroll after sending.\n        transcript.scrollTop = transcript.scrollHeight;\n        thinkingBubble.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "auto", block: "nearest" });\n\n        try {\n          // Use getAttribute because form.action is shadowed by the <input name="action"> element\n          const formAction = form.getAttribute("action") || window.location.pathname;\n          const mode = String(formData.get("mode") || "simple");\n          const language = String(formData.get("language") || "en");\n          const canonicalNextUrl = (\n            `/api/chat-ui/?mode=${encodeURIComponent(mode)}`\n            + `&language=${encodeURIComponent(language)}`\n          );\n          const response = await fetch(formAction, {\n            method: "POST",\n            body: formData,\n            headers: {\n              "X-Requested-With": "XMLHttpRequest",\n            },\n          });\n          const html = await response.text();\n          // The server may create a new conversation_id on first ask (guest or signed-in).\n          // If we don\'t carry that id into the URL, the next render defaults back to the\n          // landing state and the chat appears to "disappear" even though the thread exists.\n          let nextUrl = canonicalNextUrl;\n          try {\n            const parser = new DOMParser();\n            const doc = parser.parseFromString(html, "text/html");\n            const idCandidates = Array.from(\n              doc.querySelectorAll(\'input[name="conversation_id"]\'),\n            )\n              .map((node) => (node && node.value ? String(node.value).trim() : ""))\n              .filter((value) => value);\n            const conversationId = idCandidates[0];\n            if (conversationId) {\n              nextUrl = (\n                `/api/chat-ui/?conversation_id=${encodeURIComponent(conversationId)}`\n                + `&mode=${encodeURIComponent(mode)}`\n                + `&language=${encodeURIComponent(language)}`\n              );\n            }\n          } catch (e) {\n            nextUrl = canonicalNextUrl;\n          }\n\n          const swapped = replaceAppFromHtml(html, nextUrl);\n          if (!swapped) {\n            return;\n          }\n          // After DOM replacement, if server returned an error keep it in view,\n          // otherwise scroll to the newest assistant reply.\n          window.setTimeout(() => {\n            const serverError = document.querySelector("main.app .message.error");\n            if (serverError) {\n              serverError.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "auto", block: "nearest" });\n              return;\n            }\n            scrollToLatestAssistantInTranscript();\n          }, 50);\n        } catch (error) {\n          thinkingBubble.remove();\n          form.classList.remove("loading");\n          const currentLanguage = (\n            document.querySelector("#sidebar_language")?.value\n            || document.querySelector(\'input[name="language"]\')?.value\n            || "en"\n          );\n          const fallbackMessage = document.createElement("div");\n          fallbackMessage.className = "message error";\n          fallbackMessage.textContent = (\n            currentLanguage === "hi"\n              ? "\xe0\xa4\xb2\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa4\x87\xe0\xa4\xb5 \xe0\xa4\x89\xe0\xa4\xa4\xe0\xa5\x8d\xe0\xa4\xa4\xe0\xa4\xb0 \xe0\xa4\xb2\xe0\xa5\x8b\xe0\xa4\xa1 \xe0\xa4\xa8\xe0\xa4\xb9\xe0\xa5\x80\xe0\xa4\x82 \xe0\xa4\xb9\xe0\xa5\x8b \xe0\xa4\xb8\xe0\xa4\x95\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa5\xa4 \xe0\xa4\x95\xe0\xa5\x83\xe0\xa4\xaa\xe0\xa4\xaf\xe0\xa4\xbe \xe0\xa4\xab\xe0\xa4\xbf\xe0\xa4\xb0 \xe0\xa4\xb8\xe0\xa5\x87 \xe0\xa4\xaa\xe0\xa5\x8d\xe0\xa4\xb0\xe0\xa4\xaf\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa4\xb8 \xe0\xa4\x95\xe0\xa4\xb0\xe0\xa5\x87\xe0\xa4\x82\xe0\xa5\xa4"\n              : "The live reply failed to load. Please try again."\n          );\n          const app = document.querySelector("main.app");\n          if (app) {\n            app.prepend(fallbackMessage);\n          }\n        }\n      }\n\n      document.querySelectorAll("form.quick-submit").forEach((form) => {\n        if (form.dataset.liveAskBound === "true") {\n          return;\n        }\n        form.dataset.liveAskBound = "true";\n        form.addEventListener("submit", (event) => {\n          const actionInput = form.querySelector(\'input[name="action"]\');\n          if (!actionInput || actionInput.value !== "ask") {\n            return;\n          }\n          event.preventDefault();\n          handleLiveAsk(form);\n        });\n      });\n\n      function initConversationScrollPaging() {\n        const scrollRoot = document.querySelector("[data-conversation-scroll]");\n        if (!scrollRoot || scrollRoot.dataset.bound === "true") {\n          return;\n        }\n        scrollRoot.dataset.bound = "true";\n\n        const list = scrollRoot.querySelector("[data-conversation-list]");\n        const loading = scrollRoot.querySelector("[data-conversation-loading]");\n        const empty = scrollRoot.querySelector("[data-conversation-empty]");\n        const panel = scrollRoot.closest(".panel") || scrollRoot.parentElement;\n        const searchInput = panel?.querySelector("[data-conversation-search]");\n        const clearBtn = panel?.querySelector("[data-conversation-clear]");\n        const sortButtons = Array.from(\n          panel?.querySelectorAll("[data-conversation-sort]") || []\n        );\n        const threadStat = panel?.querySelector(\'[data-conversation-stat="threads"]\');\n        const messageStat = panel?.querySelector(\'[data-conversation-stat="messages"]\');\n        const latestStat = panel?.querySelector(\'[data-conversation-stat="latest"]\');\n        const initialItemsNode = document.getElementById("chat-ui-conversation-items");\n        if (!list) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        const language = scrollRoot.dataset.language || "en";\n        const locale = language === "hi" ? "hi-IN" : undefined;\n        const labels = language === "hi"\n          ? {\n              today: "\xe0\xa4\x86\xe0\xa4\x9c",\n              thisWeek: "\xe0\xa4\x87\xe0\xa4\xb8 \xe0\xa4\xb8\xe0\xa4\xaa\xe0\xa5\x8d\xe0\xa4\xa4\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa4\xb9",\n              earlier: "\xe0\xa4\xaa\xe0\xa5\x81\xe0\xa4\xb0\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa4\xa8\xe0\xa5\x87",\n              updated: "\xe0\xa4\x85\xe0\xa4\xaa\xe0\xa4\xa1\xe0\xa5\x87\xe0\xa4\x9f",\n              deleteLabel: "\xe0\xa4\xb9\xe0\xa4\x9f\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa4\x8f\xe0\xa4\x82",\n            }\n          : {\n              today: "Today",\n              thisWeek: "This week",\n              earlier: "Earlier",\n              updated: "Updated",\n              deleteLabel: "Delete",\n            };\n\n        let fetching = false;\n        let searchQuery = "";\n        let sortOrder = "newest";\n        let items = [];\n\n        function escapeHtml(value) {\n          return String(value || "")\n            .replaceAll("&", "&amp;")\n            .replaceAll("<", "&lt;")\n            .replaceAll(">", "&gt;");\n        }\n\n        function readJsonScript(node) {\n          if (!node || !node.textContent) {\n            return [];\n          }\n          try {\n            const parsed = JSON.parse(node.textContent);\n            return Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : [];\n          } catch (error) {\n            return [];\n          }\n        }\n\n        function getCsrfToken() {\n          const tokenInput = document.querySelector(\'[name="csrfmiddlewaretoken"]\');\n          if (tokenInput && tokenInput.value) {\n            return tokenInput.value;\n          }\n          const match = document.cookie.match(/(?:^|; )csrftoken=([^;]+)/);\n          return match ? decodeURIComponent(match[1]) : "";\n        }\n\n        function normalizeItem(item) {\n          if (!item || item.id === undefined || item.id === null) {\n            return null;\n          }\n          return {\n            ...item,\n            id: String(item.id),\n            message_count: Number(item.message_count) || 0,\n            updated_at_iso: String(item.updated_at_iso || ""),\n          };\n        }\n\n        function rowDate(item) {\n          const raw = item.updated_at_iso || "";\n          const date = raw ? new Date(raw) : new Date(0);\n          return Number.isNaN(date.getTime()) ? new Date(0) : date;\n        }\n\n        function formatShortDate(value) {\n          const date = value ? new Date(value) : new Date(0);\n          if (Number.isNaN(date.getTime()) || date.getTime() === 0) {\n            return "-";\n          }\n          return date.toLocaleDateString(locale, {\n            month: "short",\n            day: "numeric",\n          });\n        }\n\n        function updateStats() {\n          const totalMessages = items.reduce(\n            (sum, item) => sum + (Number(item.message_count) || 0),\n            0,\n          );\n          if (threadStat) {\n            threadStat.textContent = String(items.length);\n          }\n          if (messageStat) {\n            messageStat.textContent = String(totalMessages);\n          }\n          if (latestStat) {\n            latestStat.textContent = formatShortDate(items[0]?.updated_at_iso || "");\n          }\n        }\n\n        function setSortState() {\n          sortButtons.forEach((button) => {\n            const isActive = button.dataset.conversationSort === sortOrder;\n            button.classList.toggle("active", isActive);\n            button.setAttribute("aria-pressed", isActive ? "true" : "false");\n          });\n        }\n\n        function getFilteredItems() {\n          let filtered = items;\n          if (searchQuery.trim()) {\n            const query = searchQuery.trim().toLowerCase();\n            filtered = items.filter((item) => {\n              const title = String(item.title || "").toLowerCase();\n              const preview = String(item.preview || "").toLowerCase();\n              return title.includes(query) || preview.includes(query);\n            });\n          }\n          if (sortOrder === "oldest") {\n            filtered = [...filtered].reverse();\n          }\n          return filtered;\n        }\n\n        function groupItems(sourceItems) {\n          const now = new Date();\n          const startOfToday = new Date(\n            now.getFullYear(),\n            now.getMonth(),\n            now.getDate(),\n          );\n          const startOfWeek = new Date(startOfToday);\n          startOfWeek.setDate(startOfWeek.getDate() - 7);\n\n          const today = [];\n          const thisWeek = [];\n          const earlier = [];\n\n          sourceItems.forEach((item) => {\n            const updatedAt = rowDate(item);\n            if (updatedAt >= startOfToday) {\n              today.push(item);\n            } else if (updatedAt >= startOfWeek) {\n              thisWeek.push(item);\n            } else {\n              earlier.push(item);\n            }\n          });\n\n          const groups = [];\n          if (today.length) {\n            groups.push({ label: labels.today, items: today });\n          }\n          if (thisWeek.length) {\n            groups.push({ label: labels.thisWeek, items: thisWeek });\n          }\n          if (earlier.length) {\n            groups.push({ label: labels.earlier, items: earlier });\n          }\n          if (!groups.length && sourceItems.length) {\n            groups.push({ label: labels.earlier, items: [...sourceItems] });\n          }\n          return groups;\n        }\n\n        function renderCard(item, csrfToken) {\n          const mode = scrollRoot.dataset.mode || "simple";\n          const activeId = scrollRoot.dataset.activeConversationId || "";\n          const userId = scrollRoot.dataset.userId || "guest";\n          const isActive = String(item.id) === String(activeId);\n          const csrfField = csrfToken\n            ? `<input type="hidden" name="csrfmiddlewaretoken" value="${escapeHtml(csrfToken)}">`\n            : "";\n          return `\n            <div class="conversation-card${isActive ? " active" : ""}">\n              <div class="conversation-card-top">\n                <a\n                  href="/api/chat-ui/?conversation_id=${encodeURIComponent(item.id)}&mode=${encodeURIComponent(mode)}&language=${encodeURIComponent(language)}"\n                  class="conversation-link"\n                  title="${escapeHtml(item.updated_at_display)}"\n                >\n                  <span class="conversation-title">${escapeHtml(item.title)}</span>\n                  <span class="conversation-preview">${escapeHtml(item.preview)}</span>\n                  <span class="conversation-meta">\n                    <span>${escapeHtml(item.message_count_label)}</span>\n                    <span>${labels.updated} ${escapeHtml(item.updated_label)}</span>\n                  </span>\n                </a>\n                <form method="post" class="quick-submit">\n                  ${csrfField}\n                  <input type="hidden" name="action" value="delete_conversation">\n                  <input type="hidden" name="user_id" value="${escapeHtml(userId)}">\n                  <input type="hidden" name="mode" value="${escapeHtml(mode)}">\n                  <input type="hidden" name="language" value="${escapeHtml(language)}">\n                  <input type="hidden" name="conversation_id" value="${escapeHtml(item.id)}">\n                  <input type="hidden" name="active_conversation_id" value="${escapeHtml(activeId)}">\n                  <button\n                    type="submit"\n                    class="conversation-delete"\n                    title="${escapeHtml(item.updated_at_display)}"\n                  >\n                    ${labels.deleteLabel}\n                  </button>\n                </form>\n              </div>\n            </div>\n          `;\n        }\n\n        function renderList() {\n          const filteredItems = getFilteredItems();\n          const groups = groupItems(filteredItems);\n          const csrfToken = getCsrfToken();\n\n          if (clearBtn) {\n            clearBtn.hidden = !searchQuery.trim();\n          }\n          setSortState();\n          updateStats();\n\n          if (!filteredItems.length) {\n            list.innerHTML = "";\n            if (empty) {\n              empty.hidden = false;\n            }\n            return;\n          }\n\n          if (empty) {\n            empty.hidden = true;\n          }\n\n          list.innerHTML = groups.map((group) => `\n            <section class="conversation-group">\n              <div class="conversation-group-label">${escapeHtml(group.label)}</div>\n              <div class="conversation-group-items">\n                ${group.items.map((item) => renderCard(item, csrfToken)).join("")}\n              </div>\n            </section>\n          `).join("");\n        }\n\n        function mergeItems(nextItems) {\n          const seenIds = new Set(items.map((item) => String(item.id)));\n          nextItems.forEach((rawItem) => {\n            const item = normalizeItem(rawItem);\n            if (!item || seenIds.has(item.id)) {\n              return;\n            }\n            seenIds.add(item.id);\n            items.push(item);\n          });\n          renderList();\n        }\n\n        items = readJsonScript(initialItemsNode)\n          .map(normalizeItem)\n          .filter(Boolean);\n        renderList();\n\n        async function maybeLoadMore() {\n          if (fetching) {\n            return;\n          }\n          if (scrollRoot.dataset.hasMore !== "true") {\n            return;\n          }\n          if (\n            scrollRoot.scrollTop + scrollRoot.clientHeight\n            < scrollRoot.scrollHeight - 36\n          ) {\n            return;\n          }\n\n          const nextOffset = scrollRoot.dataset.nextOffset || "";\n          if (!nextOffset) {\n            scrollRoot.dataset.hasMore = "false";\n            return;\n          }\n\n          fetching = true;\n          if (loading) {\n            loading.style.display = "block";\n          }\n\n          try {\n            const mode = scrollRoot.dataset.mode || "simple";\n            const language = scrollRoot.dataset.language || "en";\n            const url = (\n              `/api/chat-ui/?fragment=conversations&offset=${encodeURIComponent(nextOffset)}`\n              + `&limit=3&mode=${encodeURIComponent(mode)}&language=${encodeURIComponent(language)}`\n            );\n            const response = await fetch(url, {\n              method: "GET",\n              headers: { "X-Requested-With": "XMLHttpRequest" },\n            });\n            if (!response.ok) {\n              throw new Error("conversation_fragment_load_failed");\n            }\n            const payload = await response.json();\n            mergeItems(payload.items || []);\n            scrollRoot.dataset.hasMore = payload.has_more ? "true" : "false";\n            scrollRoot.dataset.nextOffset = (\n              payload.next_offset === null || payload.next_offset === undefined\n                ? ""\n                : String(payload.next_offset)\n            );\n          } catch (error) {\n            scrollRoot.dataset.hasMore = "false";\n          } finally {\n            fetching = false;\n            if (loading) {\n              loading.style.display = "none";\n            }\n          }\n        }\n\n        searchInput?.addEventListener("input", (event) => {\n          searchQuery = String(event.target.value || "");\n          renderList();\n        });\n\n        clearBtn?.addEventListener("click", () => {\n          searchQuery = "";\n          if (searchInput) {\n            searchInput.value = "";\n            searchInput.focus();\n          }\n          renderList();\n        });\n\n        sortButtons.forEach((button) => {\n          button.addEventListener("click", () => {\n            const nextSort = button.dataset.conversationSort || "newest";\n            if (sortOrder === nextSort) {\n              return;\n            }\n            sortOrder = nextSort;\n            renderList();\n          });\n        });\n\n        scrollRoot.addEventListener("scroll", maybeLoadMore);\n      }\n\n      /**\n       * Fetch for same-origin routes guarded by GitaBrowseAPIPermission: browser\n       * access must not send Authorization: Token (Free plan would get 403).\n       * Always sends cookies (session) for CSRF on POST.\n       */\n      function fetchPublicBrowse(url, options = {}) {\n        const { headers: rawHeaders, ...rest } = options;\n        const h = new Headers(rawHeaders || {});\n        h.delete("Authorization");\n        return fetch(url, {\n          ...rest,\n          credentials: "same-origin",\n          headers: h,\n        });\n      }\n\n      function getChatTokenCookie() {\n        const match = document.cookie.match(/(?:^|;\\s*)chat_token=([^;]+)/);\n        return match ? decodeURIComponent(match[1]) : "";\n      }\n\n      function initConversationThreadPaging() {\n        const controls = document.querySelector(\'[data-thread-controls]\');\n        const transcript = document.querySelector(\'[data-transcript]\');\n        if (!controls || !transcript || controls.dataset.bound === \'true\') {\n          return;\n        }\n        controls.dataset.bound = \'true\';\n\n        const refreshBtn = controls.querySelector(\'[data-thread-refresh]\');\n        const loadOlderBtn = controls.querySelector(\'[data-thread-load-older]\');\n        const statusNode = controls.querySelector(\'[data-thread-status]\');\n        const conversationId = String(controls.dataset.conversationId || \'\').trim();\n        const threadLimit = Math.max(\n          parseInt(controls.dataset.threadLimit || \'30\', 10) || 30,\n          1,\n        );\n\n        if (!conversationId) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        function currentLanguage() {\n          return (\n            document.querySelector(\'#sidebar_language\')?.value\n            || document.querySelector(\'input[name="language"]\')?.value\n            || \'en\'\n          );\n        }\n\n        function setStatus(message, isError = false) {\n          if (!statusNode) {\n            return;\n          }\n          statusNode.textContent = message || \'\';\n          statusNode.classList.toggle(\'is-error\', Boolean(message && isError));\n        }\n\n        function setBusy(button, busy) {\n          if (!button) {\n            return;\n          }\n          const defaultLabel = button.dataset.labelDefault || button.textContent || \'\';\n          const loadingLabel = button.dataset.labelLoading || defaultLabel;\n          button.disabled = busy;\n          button.textContent = busy ? loadingLabel : defaultLabel;\n        }\n\n        function buildReplyPayload(content) {\n          return {\n            message: \'\',\n            guidance: String(content || \'\'),\n            response_preview: String(content || \'\'),\n            response_mode: \'fallback\',\n            verse_references: [],\n            conversation_id: conversationId,\n            language: currentLanguage(),\n          };\n        }\n\n        function buildThreadBubble(message) {\n          const language = currentLanguage();\n          const isUser = String(message?.role || \'\') === \'user\';\n          const bubble = document.createElement(\'div\');\n          bubble.className = `chat-bubble ${isUser ? (isUser) {\n            bubble.appendChild(\n              document.createTextNode(String(message?.content || \'\')),\n            );\n            return bubble;\n          }\n\n          const stack         const replyText = document.createElement(\'span\');\n          replyText.className = \'typing-text\';\n          replyText.textContent = String(message?.content || \'\');\n          replyMain.appendChild(replyText);\n          stack.appendChild(replyMain);\n\n          const shareRow = document.createElement(\'div\');\n          shareRow.className = \'reply-share-row\';\n\n          const actionsBar = document.createElement(\'div\');\n          actionsBar.className = \'reply-actions-bar\';\n          actionsBar.setAttribute(\'data-reply-actions\', \'\');\n\n          if         dislikeBtn.type = \'button\';\n            dislikeBtn.className = \'reply-act-btn act-dislike\';\n            dislikeBtn.setAttribute(\'data-reply-dislike\', \'\');\n \'same-origin\',\n              headers,\n            },\n          );\n          if (!response.ok) {\n            throw new Error(\'thread_page_fetch_failed\');\n          }\n          return scrollTranscriptToLatestReplyStart();\n              }, 40);\n            } catch (_) {\n              setBusy(refreshBtn, false);\n              setStatus(\n                currentLanguage() === Art functionality\n      function initQuoteArt() {\n        const panel = document.querySelector(\'[data-quote-art-panel]\');\n        if (!panel) return;\n\n        const styleCards =        const previewContainer = panel.querySelector(\'[data-quote-art-preview]\');\n        const previewCard = panel.querySelector(\'[data-quote-art-card]\');\n        const sanskritEl =    const featuredChips = panel.querySelectorAll(\'.featured-verse-chip\');\n\n        let currentArtData = null;\n\n        // Get CSRF token from cookie\n        function getCsrfToken() {\n          const name = \'csrftoken\';\n          let cookieValue = null;\n          if (document.cookie && document.cookie !== \'\') {\n            const cookies = document.cookie.split(\';\');\n            for (let i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {\n              const cookie = cookies[i].trim();\n              if (cookie.substring(0, name.length + 1) === (name + \'=\')) {\n                cookieValue = decodeURIComponent(cookie.substring(name.length + 1));\n                break;\n              }\n            }\n          }\n          return cookieValue;\n        }\n\n        // Style selection\n        styleCards.forEach(card => {\n          card.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n            styleCards.forEach(c => c.classList.remove(\'selected\'));\n            card.classList.add(\'selected\');\n            card.querySelector(\'input[type="radio"]\').checked = true;\n            // Regenerate if we have a verse\n            if (verseInput.value.trim() && currentArtData) {\n              generateQuoteArt();\n            }\n          });\n        });\n\n        // Featured verse chips\n        featuredChips.forEach(chip => {\n          chip.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n            verseInput.value = chip.dataset.verse;\n            generateQuoteArt();\n          });\n        });\n\n        // Generate button\n        if verseInput.addEventListener(\'keypress\', (e) => {\n            if (e.key === \'Enter\') {\n              e.preventDefault();\n              generateQuoteArt();\n            }\n          });\n        }\n\n        async function generateQuoteArt() {\n          const verse = verseInput.value.trim();\n          if (!verse) {\n            alert(\'Please enter a verse reference (e.g., 2.47)\');\n            return;\n          }\n\n          const selectedStyle = panel.querySelector(\'.style-card.selected\');\n          const style = selectedStyle ? selectedStyle.dataset.style : \'divine\';\n          const language = generateBtn.dataset.language || \'en\';\n\n          generateBtn.disabled = true;\n          generateBtn.textContent = language === \'hi\' ? \'\xe0\xa4\xac\xe0\xa4\xa8\xe0\xa4\xbe            \'Content-Type\': \'application/json\',\n            };\n            if (csrfToken) {\n              headers[\'X-CSRFToken\'] = csrfToken;\n            }\n\n            const response = await fetchPublicBrowse(\'/api/v1/quote-art/generate/\', {\n              method: \'POST\',\n              headers: headers,\n              body: JSON.stringify({\n                verse_reference: verse,\n                style: style,\n                language: language\n              })\n            });\n\n            if (!response.ok) {\n              let detail = language === \'hi\'\n                ? \'\xe0\xa4\x95\xe0\xa4\xb2\xe0\xa4\xbe \xe0\xa4\xac\xe0\xa4\xa8\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa4\xa8\xe0\xa5\x87 \xe0\xa4\xae\xe0\xa5\x87\xe0\xa4\x82               : \'Could not generate quote art. Please try again.\';\n              try {\n                const errorData = await response.json();\n                detail = (\n                  errorData.detail\n                  || errorData.message\n                  || (errorData.error && errorData.error.message)\n                  || detail\n                );\n              } catch (e) {\n                /* use default detail */\n              }\n              throw new Error(detail);\n            }\n\n            const data = await response.json();\n            currentArtData = data;\n            displayQuoteArt(data);\n          } catch (error) {\n            alert(error.message || \'An error occurred while generating quote art\');\n          } finally {\n            generateBtn.disabled = false;\n            generateBtn.textContent = language === \'hi\' ? \'\xe0\xa4\x95\xe0\xa4\xb2\xe0\xa4\xbe \xe0\xa4\xac\xe0\xa4\xa8\xe0\xa4\xbe\xe0\xa4\x8f\xe0\xa4\x82\' : \'Generate Art\';\n          }\n        }\n\n        function displayQuoteArt(data) {\n          const styleConfig = data.style;\n\n          // Apply style to preview card\n          previewCard.style.background = `linear-gradient(135deg, ${styleConfig.gradient.join(\', \')})`;\n          previewCard.style.color = styleConfig.text_color;\n\n          // Set content\n          sanskritEl.textContent = data.sanskrit_text || \'\';\n          textEl.textContent = `"${data.quote_text}"`;\n          attributionEl.textContent = `\xe2\x80\x94 ${data.attribution}`;\n          attributionEl.style.color = window.gsap.fromTo(previewContainer,\n              { opacity: 0, y: 12 },\n              { opacity: 1, y: 0, duration: 0.35, ease: \'power2.out\' }\n            );\n          }\n        }\n\n        // Copy functionality\n        if (copyBtn) {\n          copyBtn.addEventListener(\'click\', () => {\n            if (!currentArtData) return;\n            navigator.clipboard.writeText(currentArtData.share_text).then(() => {\n              const originalText = copyBtn.textContent;\n              copyBtn.textContent = \'\xe2\x9c\x93\';\n              setTimeout(() => {\n                copyBtn.textContent = originalText;\n              }, 1500);\n            });\n          });\n        }\n\n        // Share functionality\n        if (shareBtn) {\n   }, 1500);\n            }\n          });\n        }\n      }\n\n      // Gita Reader functionality\n      function initGitaReader() {\n        const openBtns = </div>\n          `;\n        }\n\n        function updateNav(view, chapterNum = null) {\n          currentView = view;\n          let navHTML = `<button type="button" class="reader-nav-item ${view }\n            function setLoadingIcon() {\n              audioBtn.innerHTML = \'<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" style="animation:spin 1s linear infinite"><path d="M12 || !container) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        function getCsrfTokenFromCookie() {\n          const name = "csrftoken";\n          if (document.cookie && document.cookie !== "") {\n            const cookies = document.cookie.split(";");\n            for (let i = 0; i < cookies.length; i++) {\n              const cookie = cookies[i].trim();\n              if (cookie.substring(0, name.length + 1) === name + "=") {\n                return decodeURIComponent(cookie.substring(name.length + 1));\n              }\n            }\n          }\n          return "";\n        }\n\n        function renderButton() {\n          if (!window.google || !window.google.accounts || !window.google.accounts.id) {\n            return false;\n          }\n          const uiLang =\n            document.body.dataset.uiLanguage ||\n            document.querySelector("#sidebar_language")?.value ||\n            document.querySelector("#nav_language")?.value ||\n            "en";\n\n          window.handleGoogleCredentialResponse = async function (response) {\n            const idToken = response && response.credential;\n            if (!idToken) {\n              return;\n            }\n            const csrf = getCsrfTokenFromCookie();\n            try {\n              const res = await fetch("/api/auth/google/", {\n                method: "POST",\n                credentials: "same-origin",\n                headers: {\n                  "Content-Type": "application/json",\n                  ...(csrf ? { "X-CSRFToken": csrf } : {}),\n                },\n                body: JSON.stringify({ id_token: idToken }),\n              });\n              if (res.ok) {\n                window.location.reload();\n                return;\n              }\n              let msg = "Google sign-in failed.";\n              try {\n                const data = await res.json();\n                const inner = data && (data.error || data.detail);\n                if (inner && typeof inner === "object" && inner.message) {\n                  msg = inner.message;\n                } else if (typeof inner === "string") {\n                  msg = inner;\n                }\n              } catch (_) {\n                /* ignore */\n              }\n              window.alert(msg);\n            } catch (_) {\n              window.alert("Google sign-in failed. Please try again.");\n            }\n          };\n\n          window.google.accounts.id.initialize({\n            client_id: clientId,\n            callback: window.handleGoogleCredentialResponse,\n            ux_mode: "popup",\n          });\n          window.google.accounts.id.renderButton(container, {\n            theme: "filled_blue",\n            size: "large",\n            text: "continue_with",\n            width: Math.min(container.offsetWidth || 360, 400),\n            locale: uiLang === "hi" ? "hi" : "en",\n          });\n          return true;\n        }\n\n        let tries = 0;\n        (function waitForGsi() {\n          if (renderButton()) {\n            return;\n          }\n          tries += 1;\n          if (tries < 80) {\n            window.setTimeout(waitForGsi, 100);\n          }\n        })();\n      }\n\n      function initGuestNavAuth() {\n        const authLinks = document.querySelectorAll(\'[data-nav-auth-target]\');\n        const overlay = document.querySelector(\'[data-auth-modal-overlay]\');\n        const modal = document.querySelector(\'[data-auth-modal]\');\n        const closeBtn = document.querySelector(\'[data-close-auth-modal]\');\n        const tabs = document.querySelectorAll(\'[data-auth-tab]\');\n        const panels = document.querySelectorAll(\'[data-auth-panel]\');\n\n        if (!authLinks.length || !overlay || !modal) {\n          return;\n        }\n\n        function setAuthMode(mode) {\n          tabs.forEach(tab => {\n            tab.classList.toggle(\'active\', tab.dataset.authTab === mode);\n          });\n          panels.forEach(panel => {\n            panel.classList.toggle(\'active\', panel.dataset.authPanel === mode);\n          });\n        }\n\n        function openAuthModal(mode) {\n          setAuthMode(mode);\n          overlay.classList.add(\'visible\');\n          modal.classList.add(\'visible\');\n          document.body.style.overflow = \'hidden\';\n\n          const focusTargets = mode === \'login\'\n            ? .find(Boolean);\n          if (field) {\n            setTimeout(() => field.focus(), 180);\n          }\n        }\n\n        function closeAuthModal() {\n          overlay.classList.remove(\'visible\');\n          modal.classList.remove(\'visible\');\n          document.body.style.overflow = \'\';\n        }\n\n        authLinks.forEach(link => {\n
